## ErwannMillon/Color-diffusion

> [!info]
> â­ 781 Â· Python Â· 2023-08-08  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/ErwannMillon/Color-diffusion)  
> `#Diffusion Model` `#Image Colorization` `#LAB Color Space` `#UNet` 
> This project uses diffusion models to colorize grayscale images by leveraging the LAB color space, where the L channel (grayscale) is preserved and only the AB color channels are noised during training. A UNet-based model denoises the color channels conditioned on the L channel and extracted grayscale features, enabling realistic color restoration for applications like photo restoration and archival imaging.
> <sub>A diffusion model to colorize black and white images</sub>

## rofl0r/proxychains-ng

> [!info]
> â­ 10,491 Â· C Â· 2026-01-11

> ProxyChains-NG is a UNIX tool that uses LD_PRELOAD to hook socket calls in dynamically linked programs, redirecting TCP traffic through SOCKS4a/5 or HTTP proxy chains. ## clarkduvall/serpy

> [!info]
> â­ 961 Â· Python Â· 2020-08-18  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/clarkduvall/serpy) Â· [Website](http://serpy.readthedocs.org/en/latest/)  
> `#Object Serialization` `#High Performance` `#Python` `#API Development` 
> serpy is a high-performance Python object serialization library designed for speed, converting complex types like Django models and custom classes into native Python types (dicts, lists, etc.) for easy JSON conversion. It outperforms marshmallow and Django REST Framework serializers by an order of magnitude, ideal for high-throughput APIs.
> <sub>ridiculously fast object serialization</sub>

## wq/html-json-forms

> [!info]
> â­ 35 Â· Python Â· 2021-01-27  
> [GitHub](https://github.com/wq/html-json-forms) Â· [Website](https://www.w3.org/TR/html-json-forms/)  
> `#HTML Form Parsing` `#Nested JSON` `#Django REST` 
> html-json-forms is a Python library implementing the (unfinalized) HTML JSON Forms spec, designed for Django REST Framework. It parses traditional HTML form fields with array-style names (e.g., items[0][name]) into nested JSON objects, enabling structured data submission while maintaining backward compatibility with legacy clients.
> <sub>Python implementation of the (inactive) HTML JSON Forms spec.</sub>
